    76	//FIXME: split the following feature into fine-grained features.
    77	
    78	// Feature: Magic Completions
    79	//
    80	// In addition to usual reference completion, rust-analyzer provides some ✨magic✨
    81	// completions as well:
    82	//
    83	// Keywords like `if`, `else` `while`, `loop` are completed with braces, and cursor
    84	// is placed at the appropriate position. Even though `if` is easy to type, you
    85	// still want to complete it, to get ` { }` for free! `return` is inserted with a
    86	// space or `;` depending on the return type of the function.
    87	//
    88	// When completing a function call, `()` are automatically inserted. If a function
    89	// takes arguments, the cursor is positioned inside the parenthesis.
    90	//
    91	// There are postfix completions, which can be triggered by typing something like
    92	// `foo().if`. The word after `.` determines postfix completion. Possible variants are:
    93	//
    94	// - `expr.if` -> `if expr {}` or `if let ... {}` for `Option` or `Result`
    95	// - `expr.match` -> `match expr {}`
    96	// - `expr.while` -> `while expr {}` or `while let ... {}` for `Option` or `Result`
    97	// - `expr.ref` -> `&expr`
    98	// - `expr.refm` -> `&mut expr`
    99	// - `expr.let` -> `let $0 = expr;`
   100	// - `expr.lete` -> `let $1 = expr else { $0 };`
   101	// - `expr.letm` -> `let mut $0 = expr;`
   102	// - `expr.not` -> `!expr`
   103	// - `expr.dbg` -> `dbg!(expr)`
   104	// - `expr.dbgr` -> `dbg!(&expr)`
   105	// - `expr.call` -> `(expr)`
   106	//
   107	// There also snippet completions:
   108	//
   109	// #### Expressions
   110	//
   111	// - `pd` -> `eprintln!(" = {:?}", );`
   112	// - `ppd` -> `eprintln!(" = {:#?}", );`
   113	//
   114	// #### Items
   115	//
   116	// - `tfn` -> `#[test] fn feature(){}`
   117	// - `tmod` ->
   118	// ```rust
   119	// #[cfg(test)]
   120	// mod tests {
   121	//     use super::*;
   122	//
   123	//     #[test]
   124	//     fn test_name() {}
   125	// }
   126	// ```
   127	//
   128	// And the auto import completions, enabled with the `rust-analyzer.completion.autoimport.enable` setting and the corresponding LSP client capabilities.
   129	// Those are the additional completion options with automatic `use` import and options from all project importable items,
   130	// fuzzy matched against the completion input.
   131	//
   132	// ![Magic Completions](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/48062697/113020667-b72ab880-917a-11eb-8778-716cf26a0eb3.gif)
   133	
   134	/// Main entry point for completion. We run completion as a two-phase process.
   135	///
   136	/// First, we look at the position and collect a so-called `CompletionContext`.
   137	/// This is a somewhat messy process, because, during completion, syntax tree is
   138	/// incomplete and can look really weird.
   139	///
   140	/// Once the context is collected, we run a series of completion routines which
   141	/// look at the context and produce completion items. One subtlety about this
   142	/// phase is that completion engine should not filter by the substring which is
   143	/// already present, it should give all possible variants for the identifier at
   144	/// the caret. In other words, for
   145	///
   146	/// ```ignore
   147	/// fn f() {
   148	///     let foo = 92;
   149	///     let _ = bar$0
   150	/// }
   151	/// ```
   152	///
   153	/// `foo` *should* be present among the completion variants. Filtering by
   154	/// identifier prefix/fuzzy match should be done higher in the stack, together
   155	/// with ordering of completions (currently this is done by the client).
   156	///
   157	/// # Speculative Completion Problem
   158	///
   159	/// There's a curious unsolved problem in the current implementation. Often, you
   160	/// want to compute completions on a *slightly different* text document.
   161	///
   162	/// In the simplest case, when the code looks like `let x = `, you want to
   163	/// insert a fake identifier to get a better syntax tree: `let x = complete_me`.
   164	///
   165	/// We do this in `CompletionContext`, and it works OK-enough for *syntax*
   166	/// analysis. However, we might want to, eg, ask for the type of `complete_me`
   167	/// variable, and that's where our current infrastructure breaks down. salsa
   168	/// doesn't allow such "phantom" inputs.
   169	///
   170	/// Another case where this would be instrumental is macro expansion. We want to
   171	/// insert a fake ident and re-expand code. There's `expand_speculative` as a
   172	/// workaround for this.
   173	///
   174	/// A different use-case is completion of injection (examples and links in doc
   175	/// comments). When computing completion for a path in a doc-comment, you want
   176	/// to inject a fake path expression into the item being documented and complete
   177	/// that.
   178	///
   179	/// IntelliJ has CodeFragment/Context infrastructure for that. You can create a
   180	/// temporary PSI node, and say that the context ("parent") of this node is some
   181	/// existing node. Asking for, eg, type of this `CodeFragment` node works
   182	/// correctly, as the underlying infrastructure makes use of contexts to do
   183	/// analysis.
   184	pub fn completions(
   185	    db: &RootDatabase,
   186	    config: &CompletionConfig<'_>,
   187	    position: FilePosition,
   188	    trigger_character: Option<char>,
   189	) -> Option<Vec<CompletionItem>> {
   190	    let (ctx, analysis) = &CompletionContext::new(db, position, config)?;
   191	    let mut completions = Completions::default();
   192	
   193	    // prevent `(` from triggering unwanted completion noise
   194	    if trigger_character == Some('(') {
   195	        if let CompletionAnalysis::NameRef(NameRefContext {
   196	            kind:
   197	                NameRefKind::Path(
   198	                    path_ctx @ PathCompletionCtx { kind: PathKind::Vis { has_in_token }, .. },
   199	                ),
   200	            ..
   201	        }) = analysis
   202	        {
   203	            completions::vis::complete_vis_path(&mut completions, ctx, path_ctx, has_in_token);
   204	        }
   205	        return Some(completions.into());
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    // when the user types a bare `_` (that is it does not belong to an identifier)
   209	    // the user might just wanted to type a `_` for type inference or pattern discarding
   210	    // so try to suppress completions in those cases
   211	    if trigger_character == Some('_')
   212	        && ctx.original_token.kind() == syntax::SyntaxKind::UNDERSCORE
   213	        && let CompletionAnalysis::NameRef(NameRefContext {
   214	            kind:
   215	                NameRefKind::Path(
   216	                    path_ctx @ PathCompletionCtx {
   217	                        kind: PathKind::Type { .. } | PathKind::Pat { .. },
   218	                        ..
   219	                    },
   220	                ),
   221	            ..
   222	        }) = analysis
   223	        && path_ctx.is_trivial_path()
   224	    {
   225	        return None;
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    {
   229	        let acc = &mut completions;
   230	
   231	        match analysis {
   232	            CompletionAnalysis::Name(name_ctx) => completions::complete_name(acc, ctx, name_ctx),
   233	            CompletionAnalysis::NameRef(name_ref_ctx) => {
   234	                completions::complete_name_ref(acc, ctx, name_ref_ctx)
   235	            }
   236	            CompletionAnalysis::Lifetime(lifetime_ctx) => {
   237	                completions::lifetime::complete_label(acc, ctx, lifetime_ctx);
   238	                completions::lifetime::complete_lifetime(acc, ctx, lifetime_ctx);
   239	            }
   240	            CompletionAnalysis::String { original, expanded: Some(expanded) } => {
   241	                completions::extern_abi::complete_extern_abi(acc, ctx, expanded);
   242	                completions::format_string::format_string(acc, ctx, original, expanded);
   243	                completions::env_vars::complete_cargo_env_vars(acc, ctx, original, expanded);
   244	            }
   245	            CompletionAnalysis::UnexpandedAttrTT {
   246	                colon_prefix,
   247	                fake_attribute_under_caret: Some(attr),
   248	                extern_crate,
   249	            } => {
   250	                completions::attribute::complete_known_attribute_input(
   251	                    acc,
   252	                    ctx,
   253	                    colon_prefix,
   254	                    attr,
   255	                    extern_crate.as_ref(),
   256	                );
   257	            }
   258	            CompletionAnalysis::UnexpandedAttrTT { .. } | CompletionAnalysis::String { .. } => (),
   259	        }
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    Some(completions.into())
   263	}
   264	
   265	/// Resolves additional completion data at the position given.
   266	/// This is used for import insertion done via completions like flyimport and custom user snippets.
   267	pub fn resolve_completion_edits(
   268	    db: &RootDatabase,
   269	    config: &CompletionConfig<'_>,
   270	    FilePosition { file_id, offset }: FilePosition,
   271	    imports: impl IntoIterator<Item = String>,
   272	) -> Option<Vec<TextEdit>> {
   273	    let _p = tracing::info_span!("resolve_completion_edits").entered();
   274	    let sema = hir::Semantics::new(db);
   275	
   276	    let editioned_file_id = sema.attach_first_edition(file_id)?;
   277	
   278	    let original_file = sema.parse(editioned_file_id);
   279	    let original_token =
   280	        syntax::AstNode::syntax(&original_file).token_at_offset(offset).left_biased()?;
   281	    let position_for_import = &original_token.parent()?;
   282	    let scope = ImportScope::find_insert_use_container(position_for_import, &sema)?;
   283	
   284	    let current_module = sema.scope(position_for_import)?.module();
   285	    let current_crate = current_module.krate();
   286	    let current_edition = current_crate.edition(db);
   287	    let new_ast = scope.clone_for_update();
   288	    let mut import_insert = TextEdit::builder();
   289	
   290	    imports.into_iter().for_each(|full_import_path| {
   291	        insert_use::insert_use(
   292	            &new_ast,
   293	            make::path_from_text_with_edition(&full_import_path, current_edition),
   294	            &config.insert_use,
   295	        );
   296	    });
   297	
   298	    diff(scope.as_syntax_node(), new_ast.as_syntax_node()).into_text_edit(&mut import_insert);
   299	    Some(vec![import_insert.finish()])
   300	}
   301

     2	
     3	use hir::{AssocItem, ScopeDef};
     4	use ide_db::syntax_helpers::suggest_name;

     8	    CompletionContext, Completions,

    12	/// Completes constants and paths in unqualified patterns.
    13	pub(crate) fn complete_pattern(
    14	    acc: &mut Completions,
    15	    ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
    16	    pattern_ctx: &PatternContext,
    17	) {
    18	    let mut add_keyword = |kw, snippet| acc.add_keyword_snippet(ctx, kw, snippet);
    19	
    20	    match pattern_ctx.parent_pat.as_ref() {
    21	        Some(Pat::RangePat(_) | Pat::BoxPat(_)) => (),
    22	        Some(Pat::RefPat(r)) => {
    23	            if r.mut_token().is_none() {
    24	                add_keyword("mut", "mut $0");
    25	            }
    26	        }
    27	        _ => {
    28	            let tok = ctx.token.text_range().start();
    29	            match (pattern_ctx.ref_token.as_ref(), pattern_ctx.mut_token.as_ref()) {
    30	                (None, None) => {
    31	                    add_keyword("ref", "ref $0");
    32	                    add_keyword("mut", "mut $0");
    33	                }
    34	                (None, Some(m)) if tok < m.text_range().start() => {
    35	                    add_keyword("ref", "ref $0");
    36	                }
    37	                (Some(r), None) if tok > r.text_range().end() => {
    38	                    add_keyword("mut", "mut $0");
    39	                }
    40	                _ => (),
    41	            }
    42	        }
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    if pattern_ctx.record_pat.is_some() {
    46	        return;
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    // Suggest name only in let-stmt and fn param
    50	    if pattern_ctx.should_suggest_name {
    51	        let mut name_generator = suggest_name::NameGenerator::default();
    52	        if let Some(suggested) = ctx
    53	            .expected_type
    54	            .as_ref()
    55	            .map(|ty| ty.strip_references())
    56	            .and_then(|ty| name_generator.for_type(&ty, ctx.db, ctx.edition))
    57	        {
    58	            acc.suggest_name(ctx, &suggested);
    59	        }
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    let refutable = pattern_ctx.refutability == PatternRefutability::Refutable;
    63	    let single_variant_enum = |enum_: hir::Enum| enum_.num_variants(ctx.db) == 1;
    64	
    65	    if let Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) =
    66	        ctx.expected_type.as_ref().and_then(|ty| ty.strip_references().as_adt())
    67	        && (refutable || single_variant_enum(e))
    68	    {
    69	        super::enum_variants_with_paths(
    70	            acc,
    71	            ctx,
    72	            e,
    73	            &pattern_ctx.impl_,
    74	            |acc, ctx, variant, path| {
    75	                acc.add_qualified_variant_pat(ctx, pattern_ctx, variant, path);
    76	            },
    77	        );
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    // FIXME: ideally, we should look at the type we are matching against and
    81	    // suggest variants + auto-imports
    82	    ctx.process_all_names(&mut |name, res, _| {
    83	        let add_simple_path = match res {
    84	            hir::ScopeDef::ModuleDef(def) => match def {
    85	                hir::ModuleDef::Adt(hir::Adt::Struct(strukt)) => {
    86	                    acc.add_struct_pat(ctx, pattern_ctx, strukt, Some(name.clone()));
    87	                    true
    88	                }
    89	                hir::ModuleDef::Variant(variant)
    90	                    if refutable || single_variant_enum(variant.parent_enum(ctx.db)) =>
    91	                {
    92	                    acc.add_variant_pat(ctx, pattern_ctx, None, variant, Some(name.clone()));
    93	                    true
    94	                }
    95	                hir::ModuleDef::Adt(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) => refutable || single_variant_enum(e),
    96	                hir::ModuleDef::Const(..) => refutable,
    97	                hir::ModuleDef::Module(..) => true,
    98	                hir::ModuleDef::Macro(mac) => mac.is_fn_like(ctx.db),
    99	                _ => false,
   100	            },
   101	            hir::ScopeDef::ImplSelfType(impl_) => match impl_.self_ty(ctx.db).as_adt() {
   102	                Some(hir::Adt::Struct(strukt)) => {
   103	                    acc.add_struct_pat(ctx, pattern_ctx, strukt, Some(name.clone()));
   104	                    true
   105	                }
   106	                Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) => refutable || single_variant_enum(e),
   107	                Some(hir::Adt::Union(_)) => true,
   108	                _ => false,
   109	            },
   110	            ScopeDef::GenericParam(hir::GenericParam::ConstParam(_)) => true,
   111	            ScopeDef::GenericParam(_)
   112	            | ScopeDef::AdtSelfType(_)
   113	            | ScopeDef::Local(_)
   114	            | ScopeDef::Label(_)
   115	            | ScopeDef::Unknown => false,
   116	        };
   117	        if add_simple_path {
   118	            acc.add_pattern_resolution(ctx, pattern_ctx, name, res);
   119	        }
   120	    });
   121	}
   122	
   123	pub(crate) fn complete_pattern_path(
   124	    acc: &mut Completions,
   125	    ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
   126	    path_ctx @ PathCompletionCtx { qualified, .. }: &PathCompletionCtx<'_>,
   127	) {
   128	    match qualified {
   129	        Qualified::With { resolution: Some(resolution), super_chain_len, .. } => {
   130	            acc.add_super_keyword(ctx, *super_chain_len);
   131	
   132	            match resolution {
   133	                hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Module(module)) => {
   134	                    let module_scope = module.scope(ctx.db, Some(ctx.module));
   135	                    for (name, def) in module_scope {
   136	                        let add_resolution = match def {
   137	                            ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Macro(mac)) => {
   138	                                mac.is_fn_like(ctx.db)
   139	                            }
   140	                            ScopeDef::ModuleDef(_) => true,
   141	                            _ => false,
   142	                        };
   143	
   144	                        if add_resolution {
   145	                            acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, def, vec![]);
   146	                        }
   147	                    }
   148	                }
   149	                res => {
   150	                    let ty = match res {
   151	                        hir::PathResolution::TypeParam(param) => param.ty(ctx.db),
   152	                        hir::PathResolution::SelfType(impl_def) => impl_def.self_ty(ctx.db),
   153	                        hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Adt(hir::Adt::Struct(s))) => {
   154	                            s.ty(ctx.db)
   155	                        }
   156	                        hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Adt(hir::Adt::Enum(e))) => {
   157	                            e.ty(ctx.db)
   158	                        }
   159	                        hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Adt(hir::Adt::Union(u))) => {
   160	                            u.ty(ctx.db)
   161	                        }
   162	                        hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::BuiltinType(ty)) => ty.ty(ctx.db),
   163	                        hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::TypeAlias(ty)) => ty.ty(ctx.db),
   164	                        _ => return,
   165	                    };
   166	
   167	                    if let Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) = ty.as_adt() {
   168	                        acc.add_enum_variants(ctx, path_ctx, e);
   169	                    }
   170	
   171	                    ctx.iterate_path_candidates(&ty, |item| match item {
   172	                        AssocItem::TypeAlias(ta) => acc.add_type_alias(ctx, ta),
   173	                        AssocItem::Const(c) => acc.add_const(ctx, c),
   174	                        _ => {}
   175	                    });
   176	                }
   177	            }
   178	        }
   179	        Qualified::Absolute => acc.add_crate_roots(ctx, path_ctx),
   180	        Qualified::No => {
   181	            // this will only be hit if there are brackets or braces, otherwise this will be parsed as an ident pattern
   182	            ctx.process_all_names(&mut |name, res, doc_aliases| {
   183	                // FIXME: we should check what kind of pattern we are in and filter accordingly
   184	                let add_completion = match res {
   185	                    ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Macro(mac)) => mac.is_fn_like(ctx.db),
   186	                    ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Adt(_)) => true,
   187	                    ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Variant(_)) => true,
   188	                    ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Module(_)) => true,
   189	                    ScopeDef::ImplSelfType(_) => true,
   190	                    _ => false,
   191	                };
   192	                if add_completion {
   193	                    acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, res, doc_aliases);
   194	                }
   195	            });
   196	
   197	            acc.add_nameref_keywords_with_colon(ctx);
   198	        }
   199	        Qualified::TypeAnchor { .. } | Qualified::With { .. } => {}
   200	    }
   201	}
   202

     1	//! Completion of names from the current scope in expression position.
     2	
     3	use std::ops::ControlFlow;
     4	
     5	use hir::{Complete, Name, PathCandidateCallback, ScopeDef, sym};
     6	use ide_db::FxHashSet;
     7	use syntax::ast;
     8	
     9	use crate::{
    10	    CompletionContext, Completions,
    11	    completions::record::add_default_update,
    12	    context::{BreakableKind, PathCompletionCtx, PathExprCtx, Qualified},
    13	};
    14	
    15	struct PathCallback<'a, F> {
    16	    ctx: &'a CompletionContext<'a>,
    17	    acc: &'a mut Completions,
    18	    add_assoc_item: F,
    19	    seen: FxHashSet<hir::AssocItem>,
    20	}
    21	
    22	impl<F> PathCandidateCallback for PathCallback<'_, F>
    23	where
    24	    F: FnMut(&mut Completions, hir::AssocItem),
    25	{
    26	    fn on_inherent_item(&mut self, item: hir::AssocItem) -> ControlFlow<()> {
    27	        if self.seen.insert(item) {
    28	            (self.add_assoc_item)(self.acc, item);
    29	        }
    30	        ControlFlow::Continue(())
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    fn on_trait_item(&mut self, item: hir::AssocItem) -> ControlFlow<()> {
    34	        // The excluded check needs to come before the `seen` test, so that if we see the same method twice,
    35	        // once as inherent and once not, we will include it.
    36	        if item.container_trait(self.ctx.db).is_none_or(|trait_| {
    37	            !self.ctx.exclude_traits.contains(&trait_)
    38	                && trait_.complete(self.ctx.db) != Complete::IgnoreMethods
    39	        }) && self.seen.insert(item)
    40	        {
    41	            (self.add_assoc_item)(self.acc, item);
    42	        }
    43	        ControlFlow::Continue(())
    44	    }
    45	}
    46	
    47	pub(crate) fn complete_expr_path(
    48	    acc: &mut Completions,
    49	    ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
    50	    path_ctx @ PathCompletionCtx { qualified, .. }: &PathCompletionCtx<'_>,
    51	    expr_ctx: &PathExprCtx<'_>,
    52	) {
    53	    let _p = tracing::info_span!("complete_expr_path").entered();
    54	    if !ctx.qualifier_ctx.none() {
    55	        return;
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    let &PathExprCtx {
    59	        in_block_expr,
    60	        in_breakable,
    61	        after_if_expr,
    62	        in_condition,
    63	        incomplete_let,
    64	        ref ref_expr_parent,
    65	        after_amp,
    66	        ref is_func_update,
    67	        ref innermost_ret_ty,
    68	        ref impl_,
    69	        in_match_guard,
    70	        ..
    71	    } = expr_ctx;
    72	
    73	    let (has_raw_token, has_const_token, has_mut_token) = ref_expr_parent
    74	        .as_ref()
    75	        .map(|it| (it.raw_token().is_some(), it.const_token().is_some(), it.mut_token().is_some()))
    76	        .unwrap_or((false, false, false));
    77	
    78	    let wants_raw_token = ref_expr_parent.is_some() && !has_raw_token && after_amp;
    79	    let wants_const_token =
    80	        ref_expr_parent.is_some() && has_raw_token && !has_const_token && !has_mut_token;
    81	    let wants_mut_token = if ref_expr_parent.is_some() {
    82	        if has_raw_token { !has_const_token && !has_mut_token } else { !has_mut_token }
    83	    } else {
    84	        false
    85	    };
    86	
    87	    let scope_def_applicable = |def| match def {
    88	        ScopeDef::GenericParam(hir::GenericParam::LifetimeParam(_)) | ScopeDef::Label(_) => false,
    89	        ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Macro(mac)) => mac.is_fn_like(ctx.db),
    90	        _ => true,
    91	    };
    92	
    93	    let add_assoc_item = |acc: &mut Completions, item| match item {
    94	        hir::AssocItem::Function(func) => acc.add_function(ctx, path_ctx, func, None),
    95	        hir::AssocItem::Const(ct) => acc.add_const(ctx, ct),
    96	        hir::AssocItem::TypeAlias(ty) => acc.add_type_alias(ctx, ty),
    97	    };
    98	
    99	    match qualified {
   100	        // We exclude associated types/consts of excluded traits here together with methods,
   101	        // even though we don't exclude them when completing in type position, because it's easier.
   102	        Qualified::TypeAnchor { ty: None, trait_: None } => ctx
   103	            .traits_in_scope()
   104	            .iter()
   105	            .copied()
   106	            .map(hir::Trait::from)
   107	            .filter(|it| {
   108	                !ctx.exclude_traits.contains(it) && it.complete(ctx.db) != Complete::IgnoreMethods
   109	            })
   110	            .flat_map(|it| it.items(ctx.sema.db))
   111	            .for_each(|item| add_assoc_item(acc, item)),
   112	        Qualified::TypeAnchor { trait_: Some(trait_), .. } => {
   113	            // Don't filter excluded traits here, user requested this specific trait.
   114	            trait_.items(ctx.sema.db).into_iter().for_each(|item| add_assoc_item(acc, item))
   115	        }
   116	        Qualified::TypeAnchor { ty: Some(ty), trait_: None } => {
   117	            if let Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) = ty.as_adt() {
   118	                cov_mark::hit!(completes_variant_through_alias);
   119	                acc.add_enum_variants(ctx, path_ctx, e);
   120	            }
   121	
   122	            ty.iterate_path_candidates_split_inherent(
   123	                ctx.db,
   124	                &ctx.scope,
   125	                &ctx.traits_in_scope(),
   126	                Some(ctx.module),
   127	                None,
   128	                PathCallback { ctx, acc, add_assoc_item, seen: FxHashSet::default() },
   129	            );
   130	
   131	            // Iterate assoc types separately
   132	            ty.iterate_assoc_items(ctx.db, ctx.krate, |item| {
   133	                if let hir::AssocItem::TypeAlias(ty) = item {
   134	                    acc.add_type_alias(ctx, ty)
   135	                }
   136	                None::<()>
   137	            });
   138	        }
   139	        Qualified::With { resolution: None, .. } => {}
   140	        Qualified::With { resolution: Some(resolution), .. } => {
   141	            // Add associated types on type parameters and `Self`.
   142	            ctx.scope.assoc_type_shorthand_candidates(resolution, |_, alias| {
   143	                acc.add_type_alias(ctx, alias);
   144	                None::<()>
   145	            });
   146	            match resolution {
   147	                hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Module(module)) => {
   148	                    let visible_from = if ctx.config.enable_private_editable {
   149	                        // Set visible_from to None so private items are returned.
   150	                        // They will be possibly filtered out in add_path_resolution()
   151	                        // via def_is_visible().
   152	                        None
   153	                    } else {
   154	                        Some(ctx.module)
   155	                    };
   156	
   157	                    let module_scope = module.scope(ctx.db, visible_from);
   158	                    for (name, def) in module_scope {
   159	                        if scope_def_applicable(def) {
   160	                            acc.add_path_resolution(
   161	                                ctx,
   162	                                path_ctx,
   163	                                name,
   164	                                def,
   165	                                ctx.doc_aliases_in_scope(def),
   166	                            );
   167	                        }
   168	                    }
   169	                }
   170	                hir::PathResolution::Def(
   171	                    def @ (hir::ModuleDef::Adt(_)
   172	                    | hir::ModuleDef::TypeAlias(_)
   173	                    | hir::ModuleDef::BuiltinType(_)),
   174	                ) => {
   175	                    let ty = match def {
   176	                        hir::ModuleDef::Adt(adt) => adt.ty(ctx.db),
   177	                        hir::ModuleDef::TypeAlias(a) => a.ty(ctx.db),
   178	                        hir::ModuleDef::BuiltinType(builtin) => {
   179	                            cov_mark::hit!(completes_primitive_assoc_const);
   180	                            builtin.ty(ctx.db)
   181	                        }
   182	                        _ => return,
   183	                    };
   184	
   185	                    if let Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) = ty.as_adt() {
   186	                        cov_mark::hit!(completes_variant_through_alias);
   187	                        acc.add_enum_variants(ctx, path_ctx, e);
   188	                    }
   189	
   190	                    // XXX: For parity with Rust bug #22519, this does not complete Ty::AssocType.
   191	                    // (where AssocType is defined on a trait, not an inherent impl)
   192	
   193	                    ty.iterate_path_candidates_split_inherent(
   194	                        ctx.db,
   195	                        &ctx.scope,
   196	                        &ctx.traits_in_scope(),
   197	                        Some(ctx.module),
   198	                        None,
   199	                        PathCallback { ctx, acc, add_assoc_item, seen: FxHashSet::default() },
   200	                    );
   201	
   202	                    // Iterate assoc types separately
   203	                    ty.iterate_assoc_items(ctx.db, ctx.krate, |item| {
   204	                        if let hir::AssocItem::TypeAlias(ty) = item {
   205	                            acc.add_type_alias(ctx, ty)
   206	                        }
   207	                        None::<()>
   208	                    });
   209	                }
   210	                hir::PathResolution::Def(hir::ModuleDef::Trait(t)) => {
   211	                    // Don't filter excluded traits here, user requested this specific trait.
   212	                    // Handles `Trait::assoc` as well as `<Ty as Trait>::assoc`.
   213	                    for item in t.items(ctx.db) {
   214	                        add_assoc_item(acc, item);
   215	                    }
   216	                }
   217	                hir::PathResolution::TypeParam(_) | hir::PathResolution::SelfType(_) => {
   218	                    let ty = match resolution {
   219	                        hir::PathResolution::TypeParam(param) => param.ty(ctx.db),
   220	                        hir::PathResolution::SelfType(impl_def) => impl_def.self_ty(ctx.db),
   221	                        _ => return,
   222	                    };
   223	
   224	                    if let Some(hir::Adt::Enum(e)) = ty.as_adt() {
   225	                        cov_mark::hit!(completes_variant_through_self);
   226	                        acc.add_enum_variants(ctx, path_ctx, e);
   227	                    }
   228	
   229	                    ty.iterate_path_candidates_split_inherent(
   230	                        ctx.db,
   231	                        &ctx.scope,
   232	                        &ctx.traits_in_scope(),
   233	                        Some(ctx.module),
   234	                        None,
   235	                        PathCallback { ctx, acc, add_assoc_item, seen: FxHashSet::default() },
   236	                    );
   237	                }
   238	                _ => (),
   239	            }
   240	        }
   241	        Qualified::Absolute => acc.add_crate_roots(ctx, path_ctx),
   242	        Qualified::No => {
   243	            acc.add_nameref_keywords_with_colon(ctx);
   244	            if let Some(adt) =
   245	                ctx.expected_type.as_ref().and_then(|ty| ty.strip_references().as_adt())
   246	            {
   247	                let self_ty = (|| ctx.sema.to_def(impl_.as_ref()?)?.self_ty(ctx.db).as_adt())();
   248	                let complete_self = self_ty == Some(adt);
   249	
   250	                match adt {
   251	                    hir::Adt::Struct(strukt) => {
   252	                        let path = ctx
   253	                            .module
   254	                            .find_path(
   255	                                ctx.db,
   256	                                hir::ModuleDef::from(strukt),
   257	                                ctx.config.import_path_config(ctx.is_nightly),
   258	                            )
   259	                            .filter(|it| it.len() > 1);
   260	
   261	                        acc.add_struct_literal(ctx, path_ctx, strukt, path, None);
   262	
   263	                        if complete_self {
   264	                            acc.add_struct_literal(
   265	                                ctx,
   266	                                path_ctx,
   267	                                strukt,
   268	                                None,
   269	                                Some(Name::new_symbol_root(sym::Self_)),
   270	                            );
   271	                        }
   272	                    }
   273	                    hir::Adt::Union(un) => {
   274	                        let path = ctx
   275	                            .module
   276	                            .find_path(
   277	                                ctx.db,
   278	                                hir::ModuleDef::from(un),
   279	                                ctx.config.import_path_config(ctx.is_nightly),
   280	                            )
   281	                            .filter(|it| it.len() > 1);
   282	
   283	                        acc.add_union_literal(ctx, un, path, None);
   284	                        if complete_self {
   285	                            acc.add_union_literal(
   286	                                ctx,
   287	                                un,
   288	                                None,
   289	                                Some(Name::new_symbol_root(sym::Self_)),
   290	                            );
   291	                        }
   292	                    }
   293	                    hir::Adt::Enum(e) => {
   294	                        super::enum_variants_with_paths(
   295	                            acc,
   296	                            ctx,
   297	                            e,
   298	                            impl_,
   299	                            |acc, ctx, variant, path| {
   300	                                acc.add_qualified_enum_variant(ctx, path_ctx, variant, path)
   301	                            },
   302	                        );
   303	                    }
   304	                }
   305	            }
   306	            ctx.process_all_names(&mut |name, def, doc_aliases| match def {
   307	                ScopeDef::ModuleDef(hir::ModuleDef::Trait(t)) => {
   308	                    let assocs = t.items_with_supertraits(ctx.db);
   309	                    match &*assocs {
   310	                        // traits with no assoc items are unusable as expressions since
   311	                        // there is no associated item path that can be constructed with them
   312	                        [] => (),

   314	                        &[_item] => acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, def, doc_aliases),

   316	                        [..] => acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, def, doc_aliases),
   317	                    }
   318	                }

   323	                        acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, def, doc_aliases)
   324	                    }
   325	                }
   326	                _ if scope_def_applicable(def) => {
   327	                    acc.add_path_resolution(ctx, path_ctx, name, def, doc_aliases)
   328	                }

   345	                            }

   347	                    };
   348	                }

    52	/// Represents an in-progress set of completions being built.
    53	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
    54	pub struct Completions {
    55	    buf: Vec<CompletionItem>,
    56	}
    57	
    58	impl From<Completions> for Vec<CompletionItem> {
    59	    fn from(val: Completions) -> Self {
    60	        val.buf
    61	    }
    62	}
    63	
    64	impl Builder {
    65	    /// Convenience method, which allows to add a freshly created completion into accumulator
    66	    /// without binding it to the variable.
    67	    pub(crate) fn add_to(self, acc: &mut Completions, db: &RootDatabase) {
    68	        acc.add(self.build(db))
    69	    }
    70	}
    71	
    72	impl Completions {
    73	    fn add(&mut self, item: CompletionItem) {
    74	        self.buf.push(item)
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    fn add_opt(&mut self, item: Option<CompletionItem>) {
    78	        if let Some(item) = item {
    79	            self.buf.push(item)
    80	        }
    81	    }

    83	    pub(crate) fn add_keyword(&mut self, ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>, keyword: &'static str) {
    84	        let item = CompletionItem::new(
    85	            CompletionItemKind::Keyword,
    86	            ctx.source_range(),
    87	            SmolStr::new_static(keyword),
    88	            ctx.edition,
    89	        );
    90	        item.add_to(self, ctx.db);
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    pub(crate) fn add_nameref_keywords_with_colon(&mut self, ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>) {
    94	        ["self::", "crate::"].into_iter().for_each(|kw| self.add_keyword(ctx, kw));
    95

    97	            self.add_keyword(ctx, "super::");
    98	        }
    99	    }

   101	    pub(crate) fn add_nameref_keywords(&mut self, ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>) {
   102	        ["self", "crate"].into_iter().for_each(|kw| self.add_keyword(ctx, kw));
   103

   109	    pub(crate) fn add_super_keyword(
   110	        &mut self,
   111	        ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
   112	        super_chain_len: Option<usize>,
   113	    ) {
   114	        if let Some(len) = super_chain_len
   115	            && len > 0
   116	            && len < ctx.depth_from_crate_root
   117	        {
   118	            self.add_keyword(ctx, "super::");
   119	        }

   121	
   122	    pub(crate) fn add_keyword_snippet_expr(
   123	        &mut self,
   124	        ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
   125	        incomplete_let: bool,
   126	        kw: &str,
   127	        snippet: &str,
   128	    ) {
   129	        let mut item =
   130	            CompletionItem::new(CompletionItemKind::Keyword, ctx.source_range(), kw, ctx.edition);
   131	
   132	        match ctx.config.snippet_cap {
   133	            Some(cap) => {
   134	                if incomplete_let && snippet.ends_with('}') {
   135	                    // complete block expression snippets with a trailing semicolon, if inside an incomplete let
   136	                    cov_mark::hit!(let_semi);
   137	                    item.insert_snippet(cap, format!("{snippet};"));
   138	                } else {
   139	                    item.insert_snippet(cap, snippet);
   140	                }
   141	            }
   142	            None => {
   143	                item.insert_text(if snippet.contains('$') { kw } else { snippet });
   144	            }
   145	        };
   146	        item.add_to(self, ctx.db);
   147	    }

   149	    pub(crate) fn add_keyword_snippet(
   150	        &mut self,

   152	        kw: &str,
   153	        snippet: &str,
   154	    ) {

   157

   160	            None => item.insert_text(if snippet.contains('$') { kw } else { snippet }),
   161	        };

   188	    pub(crate) fn add_path_resolution(

   352	        let is_private_editable = match ctx.is_visible(&func) {
   353	            Visible::Yes => false,
   354	            Visible::Editable => true,
   355	            Visible::No => return,
   356	        };
   357	        let doc_aliases = ctx.doc_aliases(&func);
   358	        self.add(
   359	            render_method(
   360	                RenderContext::new(ctx)
   361	                    .private_editable(is_private_editable)
   362	                    .doc_aliases(doc_aliases)
   363	                    .import_to_add(Some(import)),
   364	                dot_access,
   365	                None,
   366	                None,
   367	                func,
   368	            )
   369	            .build(ctx.db),
   370	        );
   371	    }

   412	    pub(crate) fn add_qualified_enum_variant(
   413	        &mut self,
   414	        ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
   415	        path_ctx: &PathCompletionCtx<'_>,
   416	        variant: hir::Variant,
   417	        path: hir::ModPath,
   418	    ) {
   419	        if !ctx.check_stability_and_hidden(variant) {
   420	            return;
   421	        }
   422	        if let Some(builder) =
   423	            render_variant_lit(RenderContext::new(ctx), path_ctx, None, variant, Some(path))
   424	        {
   425	            self.add(builder.build(ctx.db));
   426	        }
   427	    }
   428	
   429	    pub(crate) fn add_enum_variant(
   430	        &mut self,
   431	        ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
   432	        path_ctx: &PathCompletionCtx<'_>,
   433	        variant: hir::Variant,
   434	        local_name: Option<hir::Name>,
   435	    ) {
   436	        if !ctx.check_stability_and_hidden(variant) {
   437	            return;
   438	        }
   439	        if let PathCompletionCtx { kind: PathKind::Pat { pat_ctx }, .. } = path_ctx {
   440	            cov_mark::hit!(enum_variant_pattern_path);
   441	            self.add_variant_pat(ctx, pat_ctx, Some(path_ctx), variant, local_name);
   442	            return;
   443	        }
   444	
   445	        if let Some(builder) =
   446	            render_variant_lit(RenderContext::new(ctx), path_ctx, local_name, variant, None)
   447	        {
   448	            self.add(builder.build(ctx.db));
   449	        }
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    pub(crate) fn add_field(

   468	            dot_access,

   472	        );
   473	        self.add(item);
   474	    }

use ide_completion::{completions, CompletionConfig};
use ide_db::base_db::{FileId, FilePosition, SourceDatabase};
use ide_db::RootDatabase;
use syntax::{SourceFileOwner, TextRange, TextSize};
use std::sync::Arc;

fn main() {
    let code = r#"
enum State {
    Stop(()),
}

impl State {
    fn get_or_init(&mut self) -> &mut () {
        match self {
            State::Stop(_) => {
                let this = self;
                let Self::Stop(f) = this else { unreachable!() };
                *self = ;
            },
        }
    }
}
"#;

    // Create a simple database with the code
    let db = RootDatabase::default();
    let file_id = FileId(0);
    let source_db = db.file_source_database();
    source_db.set_file_text(file_id, Arc::new(code.to_string()));
    
    // Find the position where we want to complete
    let position_offset = code.find("*self = ").unwrap() + "*self = ".len();
    let position = FilePosition { file_id, offset: TextSize::from(position_offset as u32) };
    
    let config = CompletionConfig::default();
    
    if let Some(completion_items) = completions(&db, &config, position, None) {
        for item in completion_items {
            println!("Completion: {} - {:?}", item.label, item.kind);
        }
    }
}

            },

     1	//! Postfix completions, like `Ok(10).ifl$0` => `if let Ok() = Ok(10) { $0 }`.
     2	
     3	mod format_like;
     4	
     5	use base_db::SourceDatabase;
     6	use hir::{ItemInNs, Semantics};
     7	use ide_db::{
     8	    RootDatabase, SnippetCap,
     9	    documentation::{Documentation, HasDocs},
    10	    imports::insert_use::ImportScope,
    11	    text_edit::TextEdit,
    12	    ty_filter::TryEnum,
    13	};
    14	use itertools::Either;
    15	use stdx::never;
    16	use syntax::{
    17	    SyntaxKind::{BLOCK_EXPR, EXPR_STMT, FOR_EXPR, IF_EXPR, LOOP_EXPR, STMT_LIST, WHILE_EXPR},
    18	    TextRange, TextSize,
    19	    ast::{self, AstNode, AstToken},
    20	};
    21	
    22	use crate::{
    23	    CompletionItem, CompletionItemKind, CompletionRelevance, Completions, SnippetScope,
    24	    completions::postfix::format_like::add_format_like_completions,
    25	    context::{BreakableKind, CompletionContext, DotAccess, DotAccessKind},
    26	    item::{Builder, CompletionRelevancePostfixMatch},
    27	};
    28	
    29	pub(crate) fn complete_postfix(
    30	    acc: &mut Completions,
    31	    ctx: &CompletionContext<'_>,
    32	    dot_access: &DotAccess<'_>,
    33	) {
    34	    if !ctx.config.enable_postfix_completions {
    35	        return;
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    let (dot_receiver, receiver_ty, receiver_is_ambiguous_float_literal) = match dot_access {
    39	        DotAccess { receiver_ty: Some(ty), receiver: Some(it), kind, .. } => (
    40	            it,
    41	            &ty.original,
    42	            match *kind {
    43	                DotAccessKind::Field { receiver_is_ambiguous_float_literal } => {
    44	                    receiver_is_ambiguous_float_literal
    45	                }
    46	                DotAccessKind::Method { .. } => false,
    47	            },
    48	        ),
    49	        _ => return,
    50	    };
    51	    let expr_ctx = &dot_access.ctx;
    52	
    53	    let receiver_text =
    54	        get_receiver_text(&ctx.sema, dot_receiver, receiver_is_ambiguous_float_literal);
    55	
    56	    let cap = match ctx.config.snippet_cap {
    57	        Some(it) => it,
    58	        None => return,
    59	    };
    60	
    61	    let postfix_snippet = match build_postfix_snippet_builder(ctx, cap, dot_receiver) {
    62	        Some(it) => it,
    63	        None => return,
    64	    };
    65	
    66	    let cfg = ctx.config.import_path_config(ctx.is_nightly);
    67	
    68	    if let Some(drop_trait) = ctx.famous_defs().core_ops_Drop()
    69	        && receiver_ty.impls_trait(ctx.db, drop_trait, &[])
    70	        && let Some(drop_fn) = ctx.famous_defs().core_mem_drop()
    71	        && let Some(path) = ctx.module.find_path(ctx.db, ItemInNs::Values(drop_fn.into()), cfg)
    72	    {
    73	        cov_mark::hit!(postfix_drop_completion);
    74	        let mut item = postfix_snippet(
    75	            "drop",
    76	            "fn drop(&mut self)",
    77	            &format!("{path}($0{receiver_text})", path = path.display(ctx.db, ctx.edition)),
    78	        );
    79	        item.set_documentation(drop_fn.docs(ctx.db));
    80	        item.add_to(acc, ctx.db);
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    postfix_snippet("ref", "&expr", &format!("&{receiver_text}")).add_to(acc, ctx.db);
    84	    postfix_snippet("refm", "&mut expr", &format!("&mut {receiver_text}")).add_to(acc, ctx.db);
    85	    postfix_snippet("deref", "*expr", &format!("*{receiver_text}")).add_to(acc, ctx.db);
    86	
    87	    // The rest of the postfix completions create an expression that moves an argument,
    88	    // so it's better to consider references now to avoid breaking the compilation

     1	//! Renderer for patterns.
     2	
     3	use hir::{Name, StructKind, db::HirDatabase};
     4	use ide_db::{SnippetCap, documentation::HasDocs};
     5	use itertools::Itertools;
     6	use syntax::{Edition, SmolStr, ToSmolStr};
     7	
     8	use crate::{
     9	    CompletionItem, CompletionItemKind,
    10	    context::{ParamContext, ParamKind, PathCompletionCtx, PatternContext},
    11	    render::{
    12	        RenderContext,
    13	        variant::{format_literal_label, format_literal_lookup, visible_fields},
    14	    },
    15	};
    16	
    17	pub(crate) fn render_struct_pat(
    18	    ctx: RenderContext<'_>,
    19	    pattern_ctx: &PatternContext,
    20	    strukt: hir::Struct,
    21	    local_name: Option<Name>,
    22	) -> Option<CompletionItem> {
    23	    let _p = tracing::info_span!("render_struct_pat").entered();
    24	
    25	    let fields = strukt.fields(ctx.db());
    26	    let (visible_fields, fields_omitted) = visible_fields(ctx.completion, &fields, strukt)?;
    27	
    28	    if visible_fields.is_empty() {
    29	        // Matching a struct without matching its fields is pointless, unlike matching a Variant without its fields
    30	        return None;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    let name = local_name.unwrap_or_else(|| strukt.name(ctx.db()));
    34	    let (name, escaped_name) =
    35	        (name.as_str(), name.display(ctx.db(), ctx.completion.edition).to_smolstr());
    36	    let kind = strukt.kind(ctx.db());
    37	    let label = format_literal_label(name, kind, ctx.snippet_cap());
    38	    let lookup = format_literal_lookup(name, kind);
    39	    let pat = render_pat(&ctx, pattern_ctx, &escaped_name, kind, &visible_fields, fields_omitted)?;
    40	
    41	    let db = ctx.db();
    42	
    43	    Some(build_completion(ctx, label, lookup, pat, strukt, strukt.ty(db), false))
    44	}
    45	
    46	pub(crate) fn render_variant_pat(
    47	    ctx: RenderContext<'_>,
    48	    pattern_ctx: &PatternContext,
    49	    path_ctx: Option<&PathCompletionCtx<'_>>,
    50	    variant: hir::Variant,
    51	    local_name: Option<Name>,
    52	    path: Option<&hir::ModPath>,
    53	) -> Option<CompletionItem> {
    54	    let _p = tracing::info_span!("render_variant_pat").entered();
    55	
    56	    let fields = variant.fields(ctx.db());
    57	    let (visible_fields, fields_omitted) = visible_fields(ctx.completion, &fields, variant)?;
    58	    let enum_ty = variant.parent_enum(ctx.db()).ty(ctx.db());
    59	
    60	    let (name, escaped_name) = match path {
    61	        Some(path) => (
    62	            path.display_verbatim(ctx.db()).to_smolstr(),
    63	            path.display(ctx.db(), ctx.completion.edition).to_smolstr(),
    64	        ),
    65	        None => {
    66	            let name = local_name.unwrap_or_else(|| variant.name(ctx.db()));
    67	
    68	            (
    69	                name.as_str().to_smolstr(),
    70	                name.display(ctx.db(), ctx.completion.edition).to_smolstr(),
    71	            )
    72	        }
    73	    };
    74	
    75	    let (label, lookup, pat) = match path_ctx {
    76	        Some(PathCompletionCtx { has_call_parens: true, .. }) => {
    77	            (name.clone(), name, escaped_name.to_string())
    78	        }
    79	        _ => {
    80	            let kind = variant.kind(ctx.db());
    81	            let label = format_literal_label(name.as_str(), kind, ctx.snippet_cap());
    82	            let lookup = format_literal_lookup(name.as_str(), kind);
    83	            let pat = render_pat(
    84	                &ctx,
    85	                pattern_ctx,
    86	                &escaped_name,
    87	                kind,
    88	                &visible_fields,
    89	                fields_omitted,
    90	            )?;
    91	            (label, lookup, pat)
    92	        }
    93	    };
    94	
    95	    Some(build_completion(
    96	        ctx,
    97	        label,
    98	        lookup,
    99	        pat,
   100	        variant,

/// Calculate the expected type and name of the cursor position.
fn expected_type_and_name<'db>(
    sema: &Semantics<'db, RootDatabase>,
    token: &SyntaxToken,
    name_like: &ast::NameLike,
) -> (Option<Type<'db>>, Option<NameOrNameRef>) {
    let mut node = match token.parent() {
        Some(it) => it,
        None => return (None, None),
    };

    let strip_refs = |mut ty: Type<'db>| match name_like {
--
            let top_syn = match top_syn {
                Some(it) => it,
                None => return ty,
            };
            for _ in top_syn.ancestors().skip(1).map_while(ast::RefExpr::cast) {
                cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_param_ref);
                ty = ty.strip_reference();
            }
            ty
        }
        _ => ty,
    };

    let (ty, name) = loop {
        break match_ast! {
            match node {
                ast::LetStmt(it) => {
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_let_with_leading_char);
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_let_without_leading_char);
                    let ty = it.pat()
                        .and_then(|pat| sema.type_of_pat(&pat))
                        .or_else(|| it.initializer().and_then(|it| sema.type_of_expr(&it)))
                        .map(TypeInfo::original)
                        .filter(|ty| {
                            // don't infer the let type if the expr is a function,
                            // preventing parenthesis from vanishing
                            it.ty().is_some() || !ty.is_fn()
                        });
                    let name = match it.pat() {
--
                    };

                    (ty, name)
                },
                ast::LetExpr(it) => {
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_if_let_without_leading_char);
                    let ty = it.pat()
                        .and_then(|pat| sema.type_of_pat(&pat))
                        .or_else(|| it.expr().and_then(|it| sema.type_of_expr(&it)))
                        .map(TypeInfo::original);
                    (ty, None)
                },
                ast::ArgList(_) => {
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_param);
                    ActiveParameter::at_token(
                        sema,
                       token.clone(),
                    ).map(|ap| {
                        let name = ap.ident().map(NameOrNameRef::Name);
                        (Some(ap.ty), name)
                    })
                    .unwrap_or((None, None))
                },
                ast::RecordExprFieldList(it) => {
                    // wouldn't try {} be nice...
                    (|| {
                        if token.kind() == T![..]
                            ||token.prev_token().map(|t| t.kind()) == Some(T![..])
                        {
                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_func_update);
                            let record_expr = it.syntax().parent().and_then(ast::RecordExpr::cast)?;
                            let ty = sema.type_of_expr(&record_expr.into())?;
                            Some((
                                Some(ty.original),
                                None
                            ))
                        } else {
                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_without_leading_char);
                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_followed_by_comma);
                            let expr_field = previous_non_trivia_token(token.clone())?.parent().and_then(ast::RecordExprField::cast)?;
                            let (_, _, ty) = sema.resolve_record_field(&expr_field)?;
                            Some((
                                Some(ty),
                                expr_field.field_name().map(NameOrNameRef::NameRef),
                            ))
                        }
                    })().unwrap_or((None, None))
                },
                ast::RecordExprField(it) => {
                    let field_ty = sema.resolve_record_field(&it).map(|(_, _, ty)| ty);
                    let field_name = it.field_name().map(NameOrNameRef::NameRef);
                    if let Some(expr) = it.expr() {
                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_with_leading_char);
                        let ty = field_ty
                            .or_else(|| sema.type_of_expr(&expr).map(TypeInfo::original));
                        (ty, field_name)
                    } else {
                        (field_ty, field_name)
                    }
                },
                // match foo { $0 }
                // match foo { ..., pat => $0 }
                ast::MatchExpr(it) => {
                    let on_arrow = previous_non_trivia_token(token.clone()).is_some_and(|it| T![=>] == it.kind());

                    let ty = if on_arrow {
                        // match foo { ..., pat => $0 }
                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_body_without_leading_char);
                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_body_with_leading_char);
                        sema.type_of_expr(&it.into())
                    } else {
                        // match foo { $0 }
                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_without_leading_char);
                        it.expr().and_then(|e| sema.type_of_expr(&e))
                    }.map(TypeInfo::original);
                    (ty, None)
                },
                ast::IfExpr(it) => {
                    let ty = it.condition()
                        .and_then(|e| sema.type_of_expr(&e))
                        .map(TypeInfo::original);
                    (ty, None)
                },
                ast::IdentPat(it) => {
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_if_let_with_leading_char);
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_with_leading_char);
                    let ty = sema.type_of_pat(&ast::Pat::from(it)).map(TypeInfo::original);
                    (ty, None)
                },
                ast::Fn(it) => {
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_ret_with_leading_char);
                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_ret_without_leading_char);
                    let def = sema.to_def(&it);
                    (def.map(|def| def.ret_type(sema.db)), None)
                },
                ast::ClosureExpr(it) => {
                    let ty = sema.type_of_expr(&it.into());
                    ty.and_then(|ty| ty.original.as_callable(sema.db))
                        .map(|c| (Some(c.return_type()), None))
                        .unwrap_or((None, None))
                },
                ast::ParamList(_) => (None, None),

   738	
   739	fn classify_lifetime(
   740	    sema: &Semantics<'_, RootDatabase>,
   741	    original_file: &SyntaxNode,
   742	    lifetime: ast::Lifetime,
   743	) -> Option<LifetimeContext> {
   744	    let parent = lifetime.syntax().parent()?;
   745	    if parent.kind() == SyntaxKind::ERROR {
   746	        return None;
   747	    }
   748	
   749	    let lifetime =
   750	        find_node_at_offset::<ast::Lifetime>(original_file, lifetime.syntax().text_range().start());
   751	    let kind = match_ast! {
   752	        match parent {
   753	            ast::LifetimeParam(_) => LifetimeKind::LifetimeParam,
   754	            ast::BreakExpr(_) => LifetimeKind::LabelRef,
   755	            ast::ContinueExpr(_) => LifetimeKind::LabelRef,
   756	            ast::Label(_) => LifetimeKind::LabelDef,
   757	            _ => {
   758	                let def = lifetime.as_ref().and_then(|lt| sema.scope(lt.syntax())?.generic_def());
   759	                LifetimeKind::Lifetime { in_lifetime_param_bound: ast::TypeBound::can_cast(parent.kind()), def }
   760	            },
   761	        }
   762	    };
   763	
   764	    Some(LifetimeContext { kind })
   765	}
   766	
   767	fn classify_name(
   768	    sema: &Semantics<'_, RootDatabase>,
   769	    original_file: &SyntaxNode,
   770	    name: ast::Name,
   771	) -> Option<NameContext> {
   772	    let parent = name.syntax().parent()?;
   773	    let kind = match_ast! {
   774	        match parent {
   775	            ast::Const(_) => NameKind::Const,
   776	            ast::ConstParam(_) => NameKind::ConstParam,
   777	            ast::Enum(_) => NameKind::Enum,
   778	            ast::Fn(_) => NameKind::Function,
   779	            ast::IdentPat(bind_pat) => {
   780	                let mut pat_ctx = pattern_context_for(sema, original_file, bind_pat.into());
   781	                if let Some(record_field) = ast::RecordPatField::for_field_name(&name) {
   782	                    pat_ctx.record_pat = find_node_in_file_compensated(sema, original_file, &record_field.parent_record_pat());
   783	                }
   784	
   785	                NameKind::IdentPat(pat_ctx)
   786	            },
   787	            ast::MacroDef(_) => NameKind::MacroDef,
   788	            ast::MacroRules(_) => NameKind::MacroRules,
   789	            ast::Module(module) => NameKind::Module(module),
   790	            ast::RecordField(_) => NameKind::RecordField,
   791	            ast::Rename(_) => NameKind::Rename,
   792	            ast::SelfParam(_) => NameKind::SelfParam,
   793	            ast::Static(_) => NameKind::Static,
   794	            ast::Struct(_) => NameKind::Struct,
   795	            ast::Trait(_) => NameKind::Trait,
   796	            ast::TypeAlias(_) => NameKind::TypeAlias,
   797	            ast::TypeParam(_) => NameKind::TypeParam,
   798	            ast::Union(_) => NameKind::Union,
   799	            ast::Variant(_) => NameKind::Variant,
   800	            _ => return None,

Analyzing the issue...

Problem: When completing after '*self = ', rust-analyzer suggests '&mut Self::XXX'
Expected: Should suggest just 'Self::XXX' without the '&mut ' prefix

Root cause: The completion system incorrectly treats assignment expressions
as pattern contexts where '&mut' is valid, instead of expression contexts.

Solution: Need to ensure that when we're in an assignment expression context,

   609	                        .and_then(|pat| sema.type_of_pat(&pat))
   610	                        .or_else(|| it.initializer().and_then(|it| sema.type_of_expr(&it)))
   611	                        .map(TypeInfo::original)
   612	                        .filter(|ty| {
   613	                            // don't infer the let type if the expr is a function,
   614	                            // preventing parenthesis from vanishing
   615	                            it.ty().is_some() || !ty.is_fn()
   616	                        });
   617	                    let name = match it.pat() {
   618	                        Some(ast::Pat::IdentPat(ident)) => ident.name().map(NameOrNameRef::Name),
   619	                        Some(_) | None => None,
   620	                    };
   621	
   622	                    (ty, name)
   623	                },
   624	                ast::LetExpr(it) => {
   625	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_if_let_without_leading_char);
   626	                    let ty = it.pat()
   627	                        .and_then(|pat| sema.type_of_pat(&pat))
   628	                        .or_else(|| it.expr().and_then(|it| sema.type_of_expr(&it)))
   629	                        .map(TypeInfo::original);
   630	                    (ty, None)
   631	                },
   632	                ast::ArgList(_) => {
   633	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_param);
   634	                    ActiveParameter::at_token(
   635	                        sema,
   636	                       token.clone(),
   637	                    ).map(|ap| {
   638	                        let name = ap.ident().map(NameOrNameRef::Name);
   639	                        (Some(ap.ty), name)
   640	                    })
   641	                    .unwrap_or((None, None))
   642	                },
   643	                ast::RecordExprFieldList(it) => {
   644	                    // wouldn't try {} be nice...
   645	                    (|| {
   646	                        if token.kind() == T![..]
   647	                            ||token.prev_token().map(|t| t.kind()) == Some(T![..])
   648	                        {
   649	                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_func_update);
   650	                            let record_expr = it.syntax().parent().and_then(ast::RecordExpr::cast)?;
   651	                            let ty = sema.type_of_expr(&record_expr.into())?;
   652	                            Some((
   653	                                Some(ty.original),
   654	                                None
   655	                            ))
   656	                        } else {
   657	                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_without_leading_char);
   658	                            cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_followed_by_comma);
   659	                            let expr_field = previous_non_trivia_token(token.clone())?.parent().and_then(ast::RecordExprField::cast)?;
   660	                            let (_, _, ty) = sema.resolve_record_field(&expr_field)?;
   661	                            Some((
   662	                                Some(ty),
   663	                                expr_field.field_name().map(NameOrNameRef::NameRef),
   664	                            ))
   665	                        }
   666	                    })().unwrap_or((None, None))
   667	                },
   668	                ast::RecordExprField(it) => {
   669	                    let field_ty = sema.resolve_record_field(&it).map(|(_, _, ty)| ty);
   670	                    let field_name = it.field_name().map(NameOrNameRef::NameRef);
   671	                    if let Some(expr) = it.expr() {
   672	                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_struct_field_with_leading_char);
   673	                        let ty = field_ty
   674	                            .or_else(|| sema.type_of_expr(&expr).map(TypeInfo::original));
   675	                        (ty, field_name)
   676	                    } else {
   677	                        (field_ty, field_name)
   678	                    }
   679	                },
   680	                // match foo { $0 }
   681	                // match foo { ..., pat => $0 }
   682	                ast::MatchExpr(it) => {
   683	                    let on_arrow = previous_non_trivia_token(token.clone()).is_some_and(|it| T![=>] == it.kind());
   684	
   685	                    let ty = if on_arrow {
   686	                        // match foo { ..., pat => $0 }
   687	                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_body_without_leading_char);
   688	                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_body_with_leading_char);
   689	                        sema.type_of_expr(&it.into())
   690	                    } else {
   691	                        // match foo { $0 }
   692	                        cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_without_leading_char);
   693	                        it.expr().and_then(|e| sema.type_of_expr(&e))
   694	                    }.map(TypeInfo::original);
   695	                    (ty, None)
   696	                },
   697	                ast::IfExpr(it) => {
   698	                    let ty = it.condition()
   699	                        .and_then(|e| sema.type_of_expr(&e))
   700	                        .map(TypeInfo::original);
   701	                    (ty, None)
   702	                },
   703	                ast::IdentPat(it) => {
   704	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_if_let_with_leading_char);
   705	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_match_arm_with_leading_char);
   706	                    let ty = sema.type_of_pat(&ast::Pat::from(it)).map(TypeInfo::original);
   707	                    (ty, None)
   708	                },
   709	                ast::Fn(it) => {
   710	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_ret_with_leading_char);
   711	                    cov_mark::hit!(expected_type_fn_ret_without_leading_char);
   712	                    let def = sema.to_def(&it);
   713	                    (def.map(|def| def.ret_type(sema.db)), None)
   714	                },
   715	                ast::ClosureExpr(it) => {
   716	                    let ty = sema.type_of_expr(&it.into());
   717	                    ty.and_then(|ty| ty.original.as_callable(sema.db))
   718	                        .map(|c| (Some(c.return_type()), None))
   719	                        .unwrap_or((None, None))
   720	                },
   721	                ast::ParamList(_) => (None, None),
   722	                ast::Stmt(_) => (None, None),
   723	                ast::Item(_) => (None, None),
   724	                _ => {
   725	                    match node.parent() {
   726	                        Some(n) => {
   727	                            node = n;
   728	                            continue;
   729	                        },
   730	                        None => (None, None),
   731	                    }
   732	                },
   733	            }
   734	        };
   735	    };

   948	    let inbetween_body_and_decl_check = |node: SyntaxNode| {
   949	        if let Some(NodeOrToken::Node(n)) =
   950	            syntax::algo::non_trivia_sibling(node.into(), syntax::Direction::Prev)
   951	            && let Some(item) = ast::Item::cast(n)
   952	        {
   953	            let is_inbetween = match &item {
   954	                ast::Item::Const(it) => it.body().is_none() && it.semicolon_token().is_none(),
   955	                ast::Item::Enum(it) => it.variant_list().is_none(),
   956	                ast::Item::ExternBlock(it) => it.extern_item_list().is_none(),
   957	                ast::Item::Fn(it) => it.body().is_none() && it.semicolon_token().is_none(),
   958	                ast::Item::Impl(it) => it.assoc_item_list().is_none(),
   959	                ast::Item::Module(it) => it.item_list().is_none() && it.semicolon_token().is_none(),
   960	                ast::Item::Static(it) => it.body().is_none(),
   961	                ast::Item::Struct(it) => {
   962	                    it.field_list().is_none() && it.semicolon_token().is_none()
   963	                }
   964	                ast::Item::Trait(it) => it.assoc_item_list().is_none(),
   965	                ast::Item::TypeAlias(it) => it.ty().is_none() && it.semicolon_token().is_none(),
   966	                ast::Item::Union(it) => it.record_field_list().is_none(),
   967	                _ => false,
   968	            };
   969	            if is_inbetween {
   970	                return Some(item);
   971	            }
   972	        }
   973	        None
   974	    };
   975	
   976	    let generic_arg_location = |arg: ast::GenericArg| {
   977	        let mut override_location = None;
   978	        let location = find_opt_node_in_file_compensated(
   979	            sema,
   980	            original_file,
   981	            arg.syntax().parent().and_then(ast::GenericArgList::cast),
   982	        )
   983	        .map(|args| {
   984	            let mut in_trait = None;
   985	            let param = (|| {
   986	                let parent = args.syntax().parent()?;
   987	                let params = match_ast! {
   988	                    match parent {
   989	                        ast::PathSegment(segment) => {
   990	                            match sema.resolve_path(&segment.parent_path().top_path())? {
   991	                                hir::PathResolution::Def(def) => match def {
   992	                                    hir::ModuleDef::Function(func) => {
   993	                                         sema.source(func)?.value.generic_param_list()
   994	                                    }
   995	                                    hir::ModuleDef::Adt(adt) => {
   996	                                        sema.source(adt)?.value.generic_param_list()
   997	                                    }
   998	                                    hir::ModuleDef::Variant(variant) => {
   999	                                        sema.source(variant.parent_enum(sema.db))?.value.generic_param_list()
  1000	                                    }
